────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Post #1  (forum post #1532228)
Author    : swpropmaker
Date      : Jan 27, 2011 at 9:53 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Guys,

Sorry it has taken so long to post here.  I want to let everyone know that has shown concern I appreciate all the well wishers and folks that have offered help.  Truth is guys that there is nothing wrong except the fact I under estimated the Police Swing  Weds-Saturday 1500 to 0300 shift.  2010 was an absolute kick in the you know what.  As my last post indicated I lost my Resin guy to the USMC this past summer.  After working those hours I was mentally, and physically beat and worn down.  The truth is I could not keep up with trying to run a side business alone.  I have started a new position with the police department.  It’s a day shift assignment and being a creature of daylight has definitely improved my energy levels.  I am currently training a new resin guy and have been hard at work getting everything lined out to take care of past due orders.

I have contacted industry famous resin kit makers and am working to reduce the work load so kits can be offered and delivered in a timely manner.  I will be using two well known and reputable folks here on the RPF and will announce who will be doing what as soon as the agreements are made.

I will be working on several patterns now and molding a few new releases in 2011 once past due orders are filled.  I want to devote the next several weeks to clear all back logged orders.  Once complete I will announce where to get what from who for new and old studio scale models I offer.  It’s a win ..win situation for everyone.

I wanted to say this too.  The main reason I don’t come here much is that I’m like a crack addict trying to sell crack!  I mean I go to the Junk Yard and I gotta have stuff and I get out of control with my spending. I "use" more than I sell.. so to speak. In turn this causes stresses with the wife.  So that’s why I’ve always put my number and email in every post so folks can call or email me.  Hopefully once things are manageable I can control the JY addiction…

I am a studio scale junkie, They say the first obstacle to recovery is acknowledging you have a problem.  Well I admitted here to everyone.  I hope once I create a more manageable work load things will get back on track.

To those I owe.  I will be contacting you through email to inform you of steps being taken to complete your order.  Those of you that I have arrangements with (Nick, Vos) expect emails too.  All aspects of situation will be rectified in a timely manner.  Don’t hesitate in emailing me with particulars. NO one will be left hanging in the breeze. Not a single person.  I know I’ve let you down but I am a fighter and will fight back and get a hold of this. 

Priorities at the movement are

 100% past due orders.  Secondary establish reliable alternate producers for desirable kits and Third re establish a controllable situation where it’s fun again for me and folks are happy.  That’s all I’ve ever wanted. 

I cannot thank each and every one of you guys for the support and kick in the butt you have given me over the years.  Trust me.  2011 is looking good.  Past due orders are taken care of.  Work load is shared among the reliable garage kit producer community and all orders are shipped in a timely manner.  

If you are an up and coming garage kit producer and want some patterns to run… contact me at my email address or give me a call.  Maybe we can work out something out.

If it doesn’t work out... I will graciously bow out... once all past due orders are fulfilled.  I’m a big enough man to know when it causing more harm than good.

Please contact me via email sneisen@bresnan.net  or phone 303 817 9339 I’d be happy to talk with you.

Respectfully 

Steve

"I understand the anger and frustration and will not make excuses for the delays.  As indicated in my previous post I have prioritized past due outs and am shipping them out weekly.  I have contacted and made arrangements to have others in our hobby  to take over projects so that any backorders can be fulfilled in a much more timely manner.  I am working as fast as I can to deliever the owed items.  I have a list of those that I have spoken with.  Please email me and I'll let you know the status of your items....  Again guys no excuse..rest assured I'm working to clear the backlog so I can get everyone taken care of.  

Steve"

It seems like you're okay if you buy one of his kits and get in on some castings from his very first set of molds, just be very sure that he sent you everything. If you order a kit later in the game, well, good luck. If you send him reference for the promise of more reference, well, good luck. I've lost count of the number of extremely sharp and talented guys who've been burned that way.

Post #94  (forum post #1617276)
Author    : vaderdarth
Date      : Mar 31, 2011 at 12:38 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I don't believe anyone who's dealt with Steve in the past would dispute that he always comes thru in the end,  but these guys who've waited the longest are just trying to see what "the end" truly means.  He will come thru.  It's sometimes the actual process of coming thru that gets ugly.   I know you guys recall that Steve had hired a guy last year specifically who poured resin parts for him.  Steve literally blew his huge backorder list down to those few of you that still remain........and then one day...........he gets a call from his resin guy and sure enough,  the guy got deployed to Iraq or Afghanistan.  So he became a one man show again.   Recently he asked some of our SS community for help and delegated all but one of his pending projects to those friends to help him finish off this backlog.  The job kills all but a fraction of his time these days,  but he hasn't let up on the stuff he has been sending out personally since this whole thing began so long ago.  We speak every single week and sometimes daily about these backlog orders and I've watched that list shrink from about 20-30 people  to just a handful in all this time.  You guys are not privy to all the times when a mould fails or a casting doesn't meet Steve's high standards,  so you don't hear about the ordering of new rubber and new resin to correct this or that..........all you guys know is that things take a long time.  I'm sure if he was independently wealthy,  he'd make 3 moulds per each part,  but that isn't realistic.    He is making progress people.  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]

Steve emailed me to talk X-Wings in November 2001 and to ask for reference on a particular hero X-Wing as he was working on a commission build up. In exchange, he offered to send "400 pics of the 32" falcon, red 3 and the y-wing I took at the Denver Celebration on CD."

I sent Steve a disc containing about 150 closeup images of that hero X-Wing model and he wrote saying he'd already mailed his reference CD in return. Steve thanked me for the pics and later posted images of his build-up and its "100% accurate" finish, but I never actually received the reference he promised, and Steve ignored the emails and PMs I sent him asking about it. Eventually, I gave up trying.

Post #124  (forum post #1624743)
Author    : NakedBrain
Date      : Apr 5, 2011 at 3:06 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Steve and I made a deal in August of 2004.

I had a DeBoer Enterprise kit that I decided I didn't want, and after hearing that I wanted to sell it, he jumped right on it.  I delivered the kit to him personally, as I only lived 20 minutes from him.  Selling/trading price was $1650, which was what I paid for the kit from Dennis himself.

In exchange, I was to receive cash and merchandise from Steve.  He paid me $400 in cash, then I was given an ATAT Ron, kit, which we decided would be another $500 toward the DeBoer kit.  "Wheelin and Dealin," he called it.

Total: $900 out of $1650

Steve then promised me a TIE interceptor kit that he was "working on" in 2004, and said it wouldn't be more than a couple of months until it would be ready.  After years of waiting for that, and Steve getting involved in the Y-Wing, we then changed the deal for the kit to be a Y, instead of the interceptor.

After 2 more years of waiting of waiting for that to come through, Steve provided me with an old Y head that he had cast, before the design had been finalized.  That was it.

In 2006 or 07, when he was deployed, I had emailed him in frustration, and he told me he would give me a TIE kit in addition to what he owed me because I had been so patient.  Never happened, either.

I've been waiting for almost 7 years, now, for a deal that I trusted in good faith would come true.  I emailed Steve On January 25th of this year, asking him if we couldn't finally get this done and resolved.  I mentioned that I had seen that he was listing a bunch of kits for sale, and expressed interest in finishing the deal by him sending me a SS Snowspeeder he was selling.  After getting no response, I emailed him again asking if he would reply.  He responded on January 27th that he "was in training" and that he'd "take care of me" when he got back into town.

Fast forward to April 5, and still... NOTHING.

All I want is the kit I was promised, or something comparable in trade.  Obviously I'n not going to get any interest on anything for waiting so unacceptably long for this all to happen.

There's more I could add, but this covers the main issue.

Tim

Post #169  (forum post #1651591)
Author    : vaderdarth
Date      : Apr 25, 2011 at 1:02 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Scott,   Steve doesn't include brass tubing in anybody's kit.  You were sent Steve's personal kit which had barrels on it that he made himself.  All you need is to hit the hobby shop and match the tubing to Steve's original guns,  drill holes in the plastic parts and glue them in.  That's how he advises everyone to make them because it's too thin to do in just resin.  All shuttle kits need to be supplemented with brass tubing.   He sent you what you circled in your picture per your request.  Hope that helps!  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]
  If you need the actual tubing,  he'll make a set of barrels for you,  but you need to measure the diameter and lengths of those barrels as he just made that one set for himself.  You own the only two barrels that Steve ever made.  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]
    He is more than willing to take care of you man,  he sent what you circled, but apparently we are not on the same pag.  Let him know. 

 For garage kits,  it's a good thing to purchase a mini metal tubing cutter and keep plenty of metal tubing stocked.  You'll use it often.  For any gun barrels on SW kits,  you want it to be as accurate as possible so you need to replace plastic bits with metal to get them thin like the original models.  That's why he didn't even make the barrels as they would have broken in transit at that diameter. 

Hope that's helpful,

Peace man, 

Dave  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]

Post #173  (forum post #1652659)
Author    : ralphee
Date      : Apr 26, 2011 at 8:17 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Search for K&S mini tube cutter, that'll do it. It does roll the edge of the cut though, keep that in mind. TBH, i get far better results with alloy tubing with a mitre and a Razor saw.

lee
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Post #174  (forum post #1652662)
Author    : vaderdarth
Date      : Apr 26, 2011 at 8:19 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Lee is right it does roll the edge,  but it's easily fixed with the mini round rasp files especially if you are using brass or aluminum stock tubing.

Post #209  (forum post #1702915)
Author    : vaderdarth
Date      : Jun 1, 2011 at 1:12 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I'm not saying he will be limiting the quantity,  I'm saying he will limit the sales to what is on hand at the time.  That way he might sell 5 of this as they are boxed and ready to go............then in another two weeks he has 5 more or something like that.  It's all about not selling something you don't have.  Hobbyists tend to set this trap for themselves and have great intentions of meeting their demand..............but real life typically screws that up.  So the only way to avoid it is do multiple smaller runs and let the sales be dictated by what you already created........not what you will create in the future.....See???

Post #259  (forum post #1876538)
Author    : swpropmaker
Date      : Sep 9, 2011 at 12:21 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Folks,

I apologize for the delays.  I am finishing casting of the oldest project owed as indicated when I got started with the “clear the back log” project.  I have received emails wanting to know "what the hell have I been doing" so I am including that here to show what I’ve been concentrating on.  Dropship Club   This project is the oldest owed and am working on it.  I foresee completion in about two to three weeks.

I have officially entered into a partnership with Mike Salzo in effort to complete the TIE Fighter and Interceptor kit back log.  This partnership has been agreed upon and progress has already been made by Mike molding the Hull of the TIE Series.  Once Mike is ready he will notify me when the kit is ready to ship and with David’s (Vader Darth’s) help start shipping out the past due list.  I am also in negotiations with another model caster to continue some other  items as well. 

The details are this.. I will concentrate on finishing the Dropship and other past due items through whatever means necessary.  Once past due items are 100% fulfilled I will no longer cast kits for large runs.  If I choose to offer a project I will contract a reputable kit producer to handle the casting.  I plan on turning this back into a stress free hobby.  

Once again I do apologize for the delays and lack of updates you all have received/not received.  Now that I can see daylight on the current project I’m working on and the partnering with Salzo I foresee major steps in getting the back log cleared sooner than later!

Moderators.. Please feel free in calling me to discuss any specific details or questions you may have as I want this effort to be highly visible.  I promise to continue to work to satisfy this back log and deliver what is owed.

Steve

Post #279  (forum post #1911638)
Author    : mslz22
Date      : Sep 24, 2011 at 10:41 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Just a quick update for everyone...I have been cranking out tie parts for Steve over the last week or so...just a little sample below.  i have all the parts for the interceptor and i am molding the last few parts over the next day or two, including the big wing.  Right now the plan for the big wing is to do it in a harder resin than usual, on that is according to the supplier has 2x the tolerance to heat before warping, as long as it captures the fine details i will be using it, it is not warp proof, but much more warp resistant.   the only draw back is that i can likely only do 1 wing per day as it needs to really set up..... This means that once all the interceptor parts are running i should be shipping an interceptor every 2-3 days. Metal armatures for the interceptors will ship direct from steve, resin ones from me included in the kit.

Some of these tie hulls will make their way to steve and he will be filling standard tie orders.

I also will be molding up one of the newer patterns, which i have in hand here,  while tie parts are in the pressure pots.  I will let steve fill you guys in to the pattern, but i will say it's one of the most beautiful things i have ever seen!

More to come, and just to let everyone know that i am pulling triple duty right now to try and get all of this caught up....my casting obligations, my build obligations and these...so please be patient if my schedule does not quite pan out as i hope it to in regard to the interceptor shipping..

thanks

mike

Post #287  (forum post #1925237)
Author    : mslz22
Date      : Oct 1, 2011 at 3:29 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I don't have the list yet, but i should have it by the middle of the week.....

I gave the resin i mentioned above a shot yesterday and it did not work really well...for a few reasons, even though it's the slow version it started to get hot and thicken up too quickly to pour the entire wing in time.  but more than that, while it was very rigid, it was also very brittle......i foresaw many broken in transit..

Good news is i have a back up plan, I am going to use my regular slow set resin with alluminum filler, it will make it more rigid while maintaining some flexibility.  Also good news is that i may be able to run 2 wings per day....maybe. 

I hope to be shipping the first couple of kits late next week...hopefully the pace will pick up as i work out the bugs and get in a groove.

thanks

mike

Quick update, interceptor wing molds are running and so far...so good....knock on wood. I do hope to get a kit or two out this week...but it may be Monday, only because i may not have time to tie up the loose ends until the weekend...like small parts/pilots etc.

Post #325  (forum post #1955059)
Author    : swpropmaker
Date      : Oct 19, 2011 at 10:49 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I'm so happy to see the past due list getting taken care of sooner rather than later.  There has been some confussion about  Mike's and my partnership.  Mike is NOT making these kits for free.  Mikes is a super swell guy by no means would I ever let him or anyone do that.  It's my responsibility and mine alone.  I am paying Mike for every kit he ships out from the back log.  We have joined forces in effort to get caught up and then produce future releases together.  

I knew it was important to get these orders out NOW and knew I could not do it alone. Well I could have ..but it would have taken 100 years.....  so I think you will agree with me I'm going the correct route here.  I'd rather pay to have these done rather than you guys wait any longer.

Mike and I have been doing this for a long time...  TIE Standards and Heros are up next .. I'm finishing the Aliens dropship project and then I can dedicate time to round out the owed list.

Thanks for hanging in there!  Mike's work is top notch and look forward to future endevors with him!  Wanna thank Vader Darth for tracking down and itemizing everything so it's easier to get folks taken care of.  David.. thanks man you are indeed a true friend.

I am checking my PM's regularly so if you have any questions i'll do my best to answer them ASAP.

Thanks

Steve

Post #339  (forum post #1961577)
Author    : vaderdarth
Date      : Oct 23, 2011 at 8:06 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I removed the folks who requested replacement armatures,   as those were correct for the kit they purchased.  The only reason they wouldn't work is if you altered the thickness of the wing star.  If it was altered the armature would be too long.    

Steve only has the 14" armatures anyway and cannot get more in a different size.  He will be using only reinforced resin armatures from now on in the future TIE kits.  

Just do what I did,  I had already built my TIE cockpit around my armature and I used a rotozip with a cutoff wheel.  Put masking tape around my armature at the length I desired,  then simply cut it off and sanded the edges smooth.  Right Back in business!!!!  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]

Dave

We are currently building the new Hero Wing star.  Trying to get the final measurments down before we commit the kit parts on it.  As soon as thats done I will be able to mold and ship all Hero TIE's.  During the process a new TIE Standard wing will be made.  Using CAD created vintage Koolshade incoroprated to the new Hero Wing Star..    In the mean time looks like I got a couple bugs to go out and a shuttle here and there...

Shooting to have everything I can currently make out by Christmas...

Hey guys.  

Need to post a update.  As most of you know January was not a good month for me do to surgery and complications from the surgery.  Was feeling better then got bronchial pneumonia resulting back to the hospital in Feb.  I was told because of the back to back anesthesia made me more susceptible to lung problems…  

On last report I am recovering but if you have any idea how you feel with this.. there is no work being done.  I am sorry for that.  I am slowly recovering from this last bout. 

WARNING to folks casting and sanding resins!!  The doctor said I had areas in my lungs that look to be scared.  He stated it could be from the 15 years of casting resin.  He also stated sanding and breathing the non-organic resin dust may be the cause…. 

USE A CHARCOL RESPRORATOR MASK WHEN CASTING AND SANDING RESINS!!  When the lung tissue is gone it does not replace itself… so don’t do what I did all these years….  Wear your protective gear!

Propcollector,  Mark, I’ve called 2 times and have left messages for you.. please gimme a call and I can let you know the plan on the shuttle.

TIE FIGHTER guys.. like I said the pattern is done all it needs is molded and cast to complete the hero kits I have all other parts ready to go.  

TIE standard guys.. The new grown Koolshade sample will be done this week.  Once I receive it and get back into the shop it will be molded and master patterns made to create the new hero wing master..

During my time in the hospital this past time EFX sent me the prototype TIE FIGHTER!!  I put it together and it is sharp looking.. I have a buddy coming over to take pictures of it and I’ll post it here first.

All owed kits.... I will endeavor to satisfy the owed list as soon as possible.  I may hire casters to complete the list as I have done in the past to make sure these go out sooner rather than later.  Looks like due to health issues caused by the casting process and dust caused by not taking protective measures may have done permanent damage I must consider all options when it comes to continuing producing garage kits in the future.

If you are owed a kit  I will satisfy the order. Please try not to worry...  You will not be left hanging I promise you that.

Trust me I just wanna start feeling better!  Cause it sucks!  trust me!

Steve

[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]
  Seriously he's only been able to cast resin for the last couple weeks ever since his hospitalization.   It was crap timing,  but his health had to take priority.  This has nothing to do with his prior poor management and how he got here in the first place.    This is about cleaning the slate and getting back to zero so he can close the door on this part of his life.   Trust me,  he doesn't want to revisit this mess ever again after this.  He's got a great set of friends who have been working their collective azzes off to get this backlog in the history books.   He takes far more time than is necessary thanking us for helping him make all this right with you guys.   

I won't lie,  I've gotten my share of frustrated over this backlog because things do not move as quickly as I would like,  but I also acknowledge that a man can do only so much at a time and though you folks don't see a new TIE wing as progress for the backlog,   yes it does mean that the backlog guys will get a better wing than they initially paid for.  This wing is a true accomplishment and lots of great guys have worked on it to make this TIE kit freaking phenomenal.  Those of you who got the improved interceptor body,  know what I'm talking about.   This kit is gonna be pretty incredible.  I know it's been a long time in the making but the end product will be well worth the wait.   This new wing is like 30X better than the one you "almost got".  Same for the cockpit and doodads.   He's gonna unveil pics of the lab grown Koolshade to be used in this kit and your jaw will hit the floor.   These pics we've been showing illustrate what will become the standard and deluxe TIE wings.   Nothing on the market will compare.   

So guys please don't get disjointed over pics of new product,  it truly does relate to the backlog in a big big way.  If it didn't I wouldn't have posted it here.

Cool.  Have a minor update on TIE fighters:

Resin koolshade and TIE wing star master pattern have been finished and are now with  Steve.  He's sending to his mould guy who will create moulds to reproduce it for a cost effective version of the hero models for those that don't want to shell out that much dough for the real stuff.    

He will also send me the TIE wing star (new master pattern) and the resin Koolshade and I am planning on building the new standard wing,  again which will go to the mould maker as one single wing piece.  The whole wing will then be moulded in one piece and become the new standard wing.  It should look identical to the hero wings from the film.  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]
  Pics should be posted soon.   As soon as these babies get in rubber,  the TIE's will finally be finished up and shipped out and we can finish clearing this backlog.  

Dave

Post #670  (forum post #2735554)
Author    : mslz22
Date      : Feb 7, 2013 at 4:01 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

The legs will be cast with about a 20 percent fill of aluminum power, that strengthens the resin substantially, getting it close to a HDensity resin without the brittleness.   Any brass small enough to fit in the parts IMO is not thick enough to strengthen the parts.

You may still want to consider a clear acrylic tube as additional support, but you will get a better feel for that when the legs arrive.

mike

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Post #716  (forum post #2931613)
Author    : dragnink
Date      : Jun 7, 2013 at 5:19 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I think by "grown" Mike means 3d printed, it's a term used in the industry and it probably confuses a lot of people outside it.. and rightfully so, lol.

If they have seeds to grow the old Koolshade, I'd be all over it. (maybe Monsanto will figure it out, hehe)
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Post #717  (forum post #2932008)
Author    : mslz22
Date      : Jun 8, 2013 at 3:52 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Exactly correct.  The old Std Tie had the koolshade pies cast into the wing stars and were clayed up real koolshade.  The new Std tie will have 3d engineered and printed koolshade pies that will be all cast separately from the wing stars,  much, much easier to paint.  Part of the delay has been figuring out how to "print" the koolshade,  until recently the shop that Steve uses did not have a machine that could handle a 2 sided koolshade pie big enough to fit the tie.  The original idea was to "grow" a piece smaller but with an invisible interlock, mold that piece and cast it multiple times to get a piece big enough to cut the pies from, then mold those.  That had a lot of work put into it but ultimately did not work convincingly enough because of the seam and some warping on the grown part.  The new way, which has only been available since about the time of Wfest this year, should be much easier and much more convincing.

mike

dragnink said:

			I think by "grown" Mike means 3d printed, it's a term used in the industry and it probably confuses a lot of people outside it.. and rightfully so, lol.

If they have seeds to grow the old Koolshade, I'd be all over it. (maybe Monsanto will figure it out, hehe)

Post #758  (forum post #3097133)
Author    : swpropmaker
Date      : Oct 30, 2013 at 10:37 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Hey folks,

Yes the one and only Steve Neisen here.. in person.... I wanna thank Dave and Mike for helping me out this past year...   I have not sold a thing on the RPF since asking for an opportunity to get caught up on all past due orders.  A list that started this over 60 owed is down to 4.  Now it looks like folks still wanna burn me at the steak..  As far as the hold up on the TIE standard kit I hired a 3D artist to make virtual koolshade for the new standard wing. Once that's grown I will mold and master a new resin koolshade insert to be used with the new hero wing stars.   Of the TIE kits remaining I am offering to send the TIE Hero version to settle the owed list. OR email me for a refund.   Also the hero kit offer does NOT include Koolshade.  I can tell you I've stayed the course and have satisfied the majority of all owed folks. In the end no one will go without a refund or what was owed I think I've done a pretty darn good job considering the hole I got myself into... Regardless of the reasons why I fell behind...   I stayed faced the fire.. looking all my critics in the face as a man...  im not proud of what happened.. but instead of running I am finishing the list as I said I would. Those that go out of there way to back stab me behind the scenes.. flame me on the forums..  go ahead if it makes you feel better.. the fact is... I stood up and that means something and if you don't see it then there is nothing else I can do for you.  I screwed up... I admit that.  However I've taken the necessary action to fix it! With help of some members here and on my own I've addressed the situations that caused me to fall behind and have not taken any additional backlog since.  Most kits sold since (20) K'Tingas shipped the same or next day after payment was made.  Problem is no one ever writes about that.. not juicy enough.  I've reached out to those who are still owed on the list.  If you have not received an email from me please email me directly do not email Jamie or Dave.  I will personally put this backlog to bed.  Please email me if you want the hero TIE kit in exchange for the standard or anything else I make Id consider swapping for the standard kit owed.   I'll have the 3D artist post his work here on the vintage koolshade panels so you see I am truly in the process of making these new wings.  To be honest folks I miss this community.. the fellow artist that make up this forum.  The shared ideas.. ect  I was here on the rpf from the beginning...  I know getting behind pissed off a lot of folks.. I hope with my efforts to make things right people can one day forgive me and see the ways of the past are just that... the past.  I've surrounded myself with quality human beings  and have learned from their example.. that's the best I can do.. I pray that's its enough.  Look forward to your emails.

Respectfully Submitted,

Steve

AKA SWPROPMAKER
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Post #759  (forum post #3097169)
Author    : swpropmaker
Date      : Oct 30, 2013 at 11:11 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I wanted to add this bit of info for those wondering why the TIE standard kit has taken so long to ship.  Its a total re-do.  I will not send customers the old kit.  Here you see the wing size comparison.. old version on left new on right.  The new wing is larger... 

[IMAGE: 50518-c8049c4ca8224cd71d0346477f0e4b65.jpg]
 

thus the koolshade pattern I had could not be used for the resin version.  Its very time consuming to produce an accurate master of the new hero standard.  I have also changed materials used in casting.  I use a smooth on product now.  Very stable nice a clean castings.

[IMAGE: 50519-5b937db2364ec9f2e664b843901bb66a.jpg]
 

It doesn't excuse the delays but wanted to let folks know who were waiting the why.. in the end it will be the best TIE kit I've ever done and were about two-three weeks away from final product.
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I'd like to add that not only is the wing larger but both JC and I did a substantial amount of research to ID the remaining parts.  Unless you had access to the original Master used 35 years ago, this is as accurate as you will find with about 10-15 or so additional part finds.

Ok guys a lil update.. The Virtual koolshade to my understanding has been grown and will be headed my way on Monday!  Give we a week to mold and prepare the master insert then a two part mold.. 2 weeks tops...  TIE fighters will ship!!  I have the escape pod bodies cast still waiting on one address.  Thanks Dave for your hard work and George your friendly nudges are quite motivating.  We are almost finished with the back log.  I want to thank the entire studio scale community for giving me the opportunity to satisfy the backlog of orders.  As far as my business making studio scale kits... I have a dedicated climate controlled shop space now.. no outside job to interfere with development and production of studio scale and other kits.  I am full time to work on just models!  I'll do a virtual shop tour once I get the backlog list taken care of and introduce you guys to John VeValley a 30 year Hollywood professional I have working with me full time now... things are indeed looking up!!!  Also taking some advice from a close friend and will start a Nice-N Model Designs Facebook page where folks can drop in and see what's available and the work we have done past, present and future!!  I am still working close with EFX on their future studio scale releases with Gold Leader on the top of that short list.  Will update more 

as soon as I have something to report!

Post #844  (forum post #3331398)
Author    : vaderdarth
Date      : Jun 7, 2014 at 10:36 AM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Update:  I have some big news concerning Steve and the backlog.  Most of you do not know,  but Steve has been hired by the newly created Chronicle LLC.  Chronicle has secured the licenses for several movies including Robocop, Buck Rogers in the 25th Century, and several others.  They will be much like eFx and will be producing high end finished models.  Because of the license agreements,  Steve will not be able to produce any new models outside of the agreements made through Chronicle LLC. Steve has turned his TIE fighter backlog over to John Lavalley.  His company:  Rezin Nation, will complete building/moulding the TIE wing and fulfilling the remaining backlog orders.

John's contact information is:   minibuilder49@yahoo.com 

We are down to 3 individuals owed TIE fighters in this backlog thread.  I also know that there will be some folks who missed out on this thread and are owed some items,  never fear all owed still be honored.  Steve has been making kits for over 15 years so things are bound to fall through the cracks from time to time.   Anyone outside of these 3 TIE fighters will just need to contact John Lavalley.   Once these TIE fighters are shipped this backlog thread will be closed. 

 Though this feels like a door is closing to us,  I know we will be enjoying the things that Steve and Chronicle will bring to our hobby in the days to come.   I will not be returning often to the RPF for personal reasons.  I won't close my account but I won't be checking in very often after that time.  I want to leave it open so folks who know me only via the RPF can still reach me.  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]

I speak for both Steve and myself,  it has been an honor working with you fine folks of the RPF.  I know many friendships have been forged in this place and many of you are considered great friends.  I look forward to what the future brings for us.  
[IMAGE: yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7]
 

Dave

Steve, I am glad that you still come here to chime in, kudos for that. However, so that Falk does not have to take all potential flak for this, but I must say that from experience (and combined experience with a few other members with a lot of international shipping experience) it is indeed not uncommon that items aren´t scanned properly in transit.

I drop the TIE sized boxed off in a box that gets collected after close of business.  Its a called an USPS after hours drop we have here in Cheyenne.. I use On Line shipping labels so it is possible to drop off the box with out any post office personal scanning it in.  Its happened a few times as I indicated in my message above.  So I'm not sure the insinuation about it not being scanned in.  I'll agree if you drop it off with the post clerk it would be very very very unusual but that's not the case here.   It was dropped in the after hours box.  I've already contacted Falk with a back up plan there are not worries here.  He and like everyone else did will receive their items. JLinNY  yes sir your exchange wings are being done will find out when they ship out and will pm you immediately. 7 Years and 10 months... and going straight to the Junkyard* (for the warped pod, that's literally). *Nevermind that, forgot the Junkyard was now for premium members only.

Edit: If you can see the attached pictures below - received a new perfect hull (grey) from Steve, as replacement for the old warped hull (beige); took 7 years 10 months.

[IMAGE: 173202-2858d1cf1a1bd8a77f31988a37f0687b.jpg]
 
[IMAGE: 173203-e4b37b703629baa34e3247b8f7eb03e7.jpg]
 
[IMAGE: 173204-47bd47a09848137b395214fa2095b347.jpg]

Seeing as everyone and their neighbor is giving you advice, I think I earned enough patience-points to add mine to the mix:

You'll have every right to feel some to sense of accomplishment once you're done with the owed kits, but don't come out of this feeling proud and relieved - your ways made A LOT of people feel A LOT of grief these past years. I think you're the type that needs constant pressure to perform - pressure like this thread; everyone can see you getting back on track, and I think it has a lot to do with it. You can't slack off once you're done here, you need to keep the pressure on; you have a chance to evolve this from a "public/social shaming type pressure" to a "goal setting accountability type pressure". Your goal should be to continue adopting good business practices, and to never ever ever slip back to your old ways. Transparency, and making yourself accountable, publicly, is key. Start a new thread, with a link to this one; call it something along the lines of "Nice-N Model Design's Accountability Buddies"; but use it not so much as a place to report, explain, and justify hold-ups and delays - I can't speak for anyone else, but I sure am tired of those from you. Instead, use RPF members and customers as your public support group to motivate you to stay efficient in your business dealings and to keep you from falling short of your goals. State your goals publicly in that thread, announce new kit projects, delivery dates, sales and shipments made, etc.; let everyone SEE what you're doing, and how you're doing it all efficiently and transparently. Beyond the real need to address an issue, don't give any more excuses - focus on what you will do to improve or do to make things right, and say it publicly. E.g., you're late on a production delivery date you announced here? Accept you will be "reminded" in the thread; own up to the fact and thank them; propose a plan to make up for the lateness and what you will do to prevent it from happening again (hire temp help, work more hours, work less projects simultaneously, revisit delivery dates, keep a production/project calendar to prevent over-tasking yourself, etc.), then do it.

Your last few posts in December, those where you give updates and make your commitments and good practice statements public; keep doing that, for every project/deadline/sale/shipment, but in more details, for as long as you're in business.

Post #903  (forum post #3524603)

Reactions : Like — Shadowknight
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Thanks Frederic (Viceland)...  thanks for taking the time to write what you did.   Standing up.. and completing the owed list was hard.  There are some  that want to see me fail and go away.  I didn't make my commitment to satisfy past due or replacement part orders to make the nay sayers happy.  I did it because it was the right thing to do.  You have indeed shown more patience than I ever could of.  Something I've worked on during this process.  Get better in all areas. I have modeled what i do now in the image of my great friend Mike Salzo.  With his mentorship I have/am taking this as on as full time job and not a part time hobby.  I don't and will not take pre orders for kit runs ever again.  I maintain a work load that is manageable and hire help when needed.  I will not used kit sale money to pay for the run in advance.  This is where you can get into trouble fast.  Which I did.  Failed miserably.  My participation here on the RPF when the list is complete will be to enjoy watching others build and not be stressed of owing anyone anything...  Since there are other outlets for sales that protect the customer.. I think I'm gonna stick to selling kits that way.  Keeps me accountable without nasty flame threads.  Plus the Studio Scale forum is not the place to sale kits from.  Its designed to allow builders a place to talk, work and show off their creations. I will not be using it for business purposes.   Again thanks for taking the time to provide constructive suggestions all have been taken to heart.    Gan's  Viceland finally received his replacement hull so there is no need to launch a paypal claim or anything as you recommended.  However you are correct.  Future Kit sales are on hand... in that they are ready for shipment.  NO PAID PRE ORDERS!  If payment is made and the package does not arrive in the prescribed time the customer will be able to file a claim and be protected.  This has been proven effective with the non Star Wars I've done the past couple months.   Molds are being done on the re detailed TIE Hull and am casting the Virtual Koolshade patterns over the Holidays...  December was a productive month towards the future.  I hope 2015 will hold many more successes!  Happy New Year Everyone!

Accept you will be "reminded" in the thread; own up to the fact and thank them; propose a plan to make up for the lateness and what you will do to prevent it from happening again (hire temp help, work more hours, work less projects simultaneously, revisit delivery dates, keep a production/project calendar to prevent over-tasking yourself, etc.), then do it.

Your last few posts in December, those where you give updates and make your commitments and good practice statements public; keep doing that, for every project/deadline/sale/shipment, but in more details, for as long as you're in business.
		

Click to expand...

Waynemo,   I should have your Y wing  kit ready to ship by Monday

Just to clarify what is going on with the Y wing at this point,  I just finished a whole new set of molds from parts that were further refined than the molds that Steve has,  thus the improvements that Steve has been talking about.  I made a number of improvements so that there will not be issues with engines being out of round and have refined a number of other parts.  Jason has also contributed a few new pattern parts,  so the new kit will be a nice improvement over the last.

Additionally this next release will have a full metal armature,  both crossbar and spine armatures,  no resin hybrid.  Now that i have a proper milling machine i can do those.

All kits will be cast and shipped directly from me.

Molds are done and ready,  I had to make some archival castings,  but those are all done and production has begun on these.

thanks

mike

Post #1026  (forum post #4206823)
Author    : madcow0812
Date      : Mar 12, 2017 at 5:51 PM
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

I just ordered the Y-wing and just noticed in the instructions I have to order some parts from Plastruct. Is this true ? and what does this mean ???You also need Plastruct tube XXXXXX for the thruster assemblies. Does this mean that some of the parts are the piping and I will have to bend it ?

In addition, you will need to purchase 8 

1/4” ABS TEE from Plastruct, code number T-8. It is easiest to order two of their 4-packs, catalog code #90086.

You will also need to puchase butyrate coated wire and butyrate tubing from Plastruct as well. I used the following catalog code tubes/wires: 90101,

90102, 90103, 90104, 90105. You also need Plastruct tube XXXXXX for the thruster assemblies. I also replaced the torpedo tubes and laser cannons with

brass tubing - that is optional, and crazy.
